posted:Posted August 4, 2023
msg:It is rare to pass by Jinzhou and choose the only five-star hotel in Jinzhou. Arrived after 6:00 pm, because it was a family of three and was directly upgraded to the executive floor. The room is big enough and the hygiene is good. The service attitude is also very serious and efficient, which is worthy of the Sheraton brand.
There are also a few regrets:
1. When taking a bath, I found that there was no bath salt. After inquiry, it was not replenished recently;
2. The ground free parking lot is basically unmanaged and somewhat chaotic;
3. Breakfast is 98 per person, the croissant is very average, other pastry bread is so-so, and the preserved egg and lean meat porridge is relatively thin.
In short, the service is very good, and there is room for improvement in hardware support.

msg:At around 2pm on the 29th, I stayed at the Sheraton Jinzhou and booked 2 rooms. The car was parked on the ground. The design of the hotel is very distinctive. It is hollow. Looking from the opposite side, there are golden ears of wheat on the ground. People who are afraid of heights stick to the room all the time. Walking... I found that the carpet under my feet is a wheat-like plant pattern, so beautiful!
The rooms are ok, clean and tidy, although there are not many, but the bathroom and toilet are separated by 2 sliding glass doors, and the privacy can also be satisfied.
I can't understand the air conditioner settings, but fortunately there is no noise at night and it is neither too hot nor too cold.
But the sound insulation is average. When sleeping in the middle of the night, the child next door is crying, which is obvious. Breakfast the next day, 2 plates of food and coffee, less than half eaten, went to get other food, came back with an empty table...
Check out is fast and the service is friendly. Didn't go to the pool etc.
